Remove deprecated ProvisioningRequest annotations
<!-- Please only use this template for submitting clean up requests -->

**What would you like to be cleaned**:
Since [this PR](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/2726), we started supporting the new ProvisioningRequest annotations, but we did not remove deprecated annotations so that we can maintain backward compatibility with the previous ClusterAutoscaler versions.

So, based on the Kubernetes deprecation policy, as we discussed [here](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/2726#discussion_r1697928601), we would like to stop using deprecated ProvisioningRequest annotations here:

    59	        objNameMaxPrefixLength = 252 - objNameHashLength

    71	type provisioningConfigHelper = admissioncheck.ConfigHelper[*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig, kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig]
    72	
    73	func newProvisioningConfigHelper(c client.Client) (*provisioningConfigHelper, error) {
    74	        return admissioncheck.NewConfigHelper[*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig](c)
    75	}
    76	
    77	type Controller struct {
    78	        client client.Client
    79	        record record.EventRecorder
    80	        helper *provisioningConfigHelper
    81	        clock  clock.Clock
    82	}
    83	
    84	type workloadInfo struct {
    85	        checkStates  []kueue.AdmissionCheckState
    86	        requeueState *kueue.RequeueState
    87	}
    88	
    89	var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*Controller)(nil)
    90	
    91	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=events,verbs=create;watch;update
    92	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=podtemplates,verbs=get;list;watch;create;delete;update
    93	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=autoscaling.x-k8s.io,resources=provisioningrequests,verbs=get;list;watch;create;update;patch;delete
    94	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=autoscaling.x-k8s.io,resources=provisioningrequests/status,verbs=get
    95	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;update;patch;delete
    96	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;update;patch
    97	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=admissionchecks,verbs=get;list;watch
    98	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=provisioningrequestconfigs,verbs=get;list;watch
    99	
   100	func NewController(client client.Client, record record.EventRecorder) (*Controller, error) {
   101	        helper, err := newProvisioningConfigHelper(client)
   102	        if err != nil {
   103	                return nil, err
   104	        }
   105	        return &Controller{
   106	                client: client,
   107	                record: record,
   108	                helper: helper,
   109	                clock:  realClock,
   110	        }, nil
   111	}
   112	
   113	// Reconcile performs a full reconciliation for the object referred to by the Request.
   114	// The Controller will requeue the Request to be processed again if an error is non-nil or
   115	// Result.Requeue is true, otherwise upon completion it will remove the work from the queue.
   116	func (c *Controller) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req reconcile.Request) (reconcile.Result, error) {
   117	        wl := &kueue.Workload{}
   118	
   119	        err := c.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, wl)
   120	        if err != nil {
   121	                return reconcile.Result{}, client.IgnoreNotFound(err)
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
   125	        log.V(2).Info("Reconcile Workload")
   126	
   127	        if !workload.HasQuotaReservation(wl) || workload.IsFinished(wl) || workload.IsEvicted(wl) {
   128	                return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        provReqs := &autoscaling.ProvisioningRequestList{}
   132	        if err := c.client.List(ctx, provReqs, client.InNamespace(wl.Namespace), client.MatchingFields{RequestsOwnedByWorkloadKey: wl.Name}); client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
   133	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        // get the lists of relevant checks
   137	        relevantChecks, err := admissioncheck.FilterForController(ctx, c.client, wl.Status.AdmissionChecks, kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName)
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        checkConfig := make(map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig, len(relevantChecks))
   143	        for _, checkName := range relevantChecks {
   144	                prc, err := c.helper.ConfigForAdmissionCheck(ctx, checkName)
   145	                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
   146	                        return reconcile.Result{}, err
   147	                }
   148	                checkConfig[checkName] = prc
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        activeOrLastPRForChecks := c.activeOrLastPRForChecks(ctx, wl, checkConfig, provReqs.Items)
   152	
   153	        wlInfo := workloadInfo{
   154	                checkStates: make([]kueue.AdmissionCheckState, 0),
   155	        }
   156	        err = c.syncCheckStates(ctx, wl, &wlInfo, checkConfig, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
   157	        if err != nil {
   158	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        err = c.deleteUnusedProvisioningRequests(ctx, provReqs.Items, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
   162	        if err != nil {
   163	                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed to delete unused provisioning requests")
   164	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   165	        }
   166	
   167	        err = c.syncOwnedProvisionRequest(ctx, wl, &wlInfo, checkConfig, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
   168	        if err != nil {
   169	                // this can also delete unneeded checks
   170	                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed")
   171	                return reconcile.Result{}, err
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
   175	}
   176	
   177	func (c *Controller) activeOrLastPRForChecks(
   178	        ctx context.Context,
   179	        wl *kueue.Workload,
   180	        checkConfig map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig,
   181	        ownedPRs []autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest,
   182	) map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest {
   183	        activeOrLastPRForChecks := make(map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest)
   184	        log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
   185	        for checkName, prc := range checkConfig {
   186	                if prc == nil {
   187	                        continue
   188	                }
   189	                for i := range ownedPRs {
   190	                        req := &ownedPRs[i]
   191	                        // PRs relevant for the admission check
   192	                        if matchesWorkloadAndCheck(req, wl.Name, checkName) {
   193	                                if c.reqIsNeeded(wl, prc) && provReqSyncedWithConfig(req, prc) {
   194	                                        currPr, exists := activeOrLastPRForChecks[checkName]
   195	                                        if !exists || getAttempt(log, currPr, wl.Name, checkName) < getAttempt(log, req, wl.Name, checkName) {
   196	                                                activeOrLastPRForChecks[checkName] = req
   197	                                        }
   198	                                }
   199	                        }
   200	                }
   201	        }
   202	        return activeOrLastPRForChecks
   203	}
   204	
   205	func (c *Controller) deleteUnusedProvisioningRequests(ctx context.Context, ownedPRs []autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest, activeOrLastPRForChecks map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest) error {
   206	        log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
   207	        prNames := sets.New[string]()
   208	        for _, pr := range activeOrLastPRForChecks {
   209	                prNames.Insert(pr.Name)
   210	        }
   211	        for _, pr := range ownedPRs {
   212	                req := &pr
   213	                if !prNames.Has(req.Name) {
   214	                        if err := c.client.Delete(ctx, req); client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
   215	                                log.V(5).Error(err, "deleting the request", "req", klog.KObj(req))
   216	                                return err
   217	                        }
   218	                }
   219	        }
   220	        return nil
   221	}
   222	
   223	func (c *Controller) syncOwnedProvisionRequest(
   224	        ctx context.Context,
   225	        wl *kueue.Workload,
   226	        wlInfo *workloadInfo,
   227	        checkConfig map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig,
   228	        activeOrLastPRForChecks map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest,
   229	) error {
   230	        log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
   231	        for checkName, prc := range checkConfig {
   232	                if prc == nil {
   233	                        // the check is not active
   234	                        continue
   235	                }
   236	                if !c.reqIsNeeded(wl, prc) {
   237	                        continue
   238	                }
   239	                ac := workload.FindAdmissionCheck(wlInfo.checkStates, checkName)
   240	                if ac != nil && ac.State == kueue.CheckStateReady {
   241	                        log.V(2).Info("Skip syncing of the ProvReq for admission check which is Ready", "workload", klog.KObj(wl), "admissionCheck", checkName)
   242	                        continue
   243	                }
   244	
   245	                req, exists := activeOrLastPRForChecks[checkName]
   246	                attempt := int32(1)
   247	                shouldCreatePr := false
   248	                if exists {
   249	                        if (isFailed(req) || (isBookingExpired(req) && !workload.IsAdmitted(wl))) &&
   250	                                // if the workload is Admitted we don't want to retry on BookingExpired
   251	                                ac != nil && ac.State == kueue.CheckStatePending {
   252	                                // if the workload is in Retry/Rejected state we don't create another ProvReq
   253	                                attempt = getAttempt(log, req, wl.Name, checkName)
   254	                                shouldCreatePr = true
   255	                                attempt++
   256	                        }
   257	                } else {
   258	                        shouldCreatePr = true
   259	                }
   260	                requestName := ProvisioningRequestName(wl.Name, checkName, attempt)
   261	                if shouldCreatePr {
   262	                        log.V(3).Info("Creating ProvisioningRequest", "requestName", requestName, "attempt", attempt)
   263	                        req = &autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest{
   264	                                ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
   265	                                        Name:      requestName,
   266	                                        Namespace: wl.Namespace,
   267	                                        Labels: map[string]string{
   268	                                                constants.ManagedByKueueLabelKey: constants.ManagedByKueueLabelValue,
   269	                                        },
   270	                                },
   271	                                Spec: autoscaling.ProvisioningRequestSpec{
   272	                                        ProvisioningClassName: prc.Spec.ProvisioningClassName,
   273	                                        Parameters:            parametersKueueToProvisioning(prc.Spec.Parameters),
   274	                                },
   275	                        }
   276	                        passProvReqParams(wl, req)
   277	
   278	                        mergedPodSets, err := mergePodSets(wl, &prc.Spec)
   279	                        if err != nil {
   280	                                return err
   281	                        }
   282	
   283	                        for _, mergedPodSet := range mergedPodSets {
   284	                                ptName := getProvisioningRequestPodTemplateName(requestName, mergedPodSet.Name)
   285	
   286	                                pt := &corev1.PodTemplate{}
   287	                                err := c.client.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Namespace: wl.Namespace, Name: ptName}, pt)
   288	                                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
   289	                                        return err
   290	                                }
   291	                                if err != nil {
   292	                                        // it's a not found, so create it
   293	                                        _, err := c.createPodTemplate(ctx, wl, ptName, mergedPodSet.PodSet, mergedPodSet.PodSetAssignment)
   294	                                        if err != nil {
   295	                                                msg := fmt.Sprintf("Error creating PodTemplate %q: %v", ptName, err)
   296	                                                return c.handleError(ctx, wl, ac, msg, err)
   297	                                        }
   298	                                }
   299	
   300	                                req.Spec.PodSets = append(req.Spec.PodSets, autoscaling.PodSet{
   301	                                        PodTemplateRef: autoscaling.Reference{
   302	                                                Name: ptName,
   303	                                        },
   304	                                        Count: mergedPodSet.Count,
   305	                                })
   306	                        }
   307	
   308	                        if err := ctrl.SetControllerReference(wl, req, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
   309	                                return err
   310	                        }
   311	
   312	                        if err := c.client.Create(ctx, req); err != nil {
   313	                                msg := fmt.Sprintf("Error creating ProvisioningRequest %q: %v", requestName, err)
   314	                                return c.handleError(ctx, wl, ac, msg, err)
   315	                        }
   316	                        c.record.Eventf(wl, corev1.EventTypeNormal, "ProvisioningRequestCreated", "Created ProvisioningRequest: %q", req.Name)
   317	                        activeOrLastPRForChecks[checkName] = req
   318	                }
   319	                if err := c.syncProvisionRequestsPodTemplates(ctx, wl, req); err != nil {
   320	                        return err
   321	                }
   322	        }
   323	        return nil
   324	}
   325	
   326	func (c *Controller) handleError(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, ac *kueue.AdmissionCheckState, msg string, err error) error {
   327	        c.record.Eventf(wl, corev1.EventTypeWarning, "FailedCreate", api.TruncateEventMessage(msg))
   328	
   329	        ac.Message = api.TruncateConditionMessage(msg)
   330	        wlPatch := workload.BaseSSAWorkload(wl, true)
   331	        workload.SetAdmissionCheckState(&wlPatch.Status.AdmissionChecks, *ac, c.clock)
   332	
   333	        patchErr := c.client.Status().Patch(
   334	                ctx, wlPatch, client.Apply,
   335	                client.FieldOwner(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName),
   336	                client.ForceOwnership,
   337	        )
   338	
   339	        return errors.Join(err, patchErr)
   340	}
   341	
   342	func (c *Controller) createPodTemplate(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, name string, ps *kueue.PodSet, psa *kueue.PodSetAssignment) (*corev1.PodTemplate, error) {
   343	        newPt := &corev1.PodTemplate{
   344	                ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
   345	                        Name:      name,
   346	                        Namespace: wl.Namespace,
   347	                        Labels: map[string]string{
   348	                                constants.ManagedByKueueLabelKey: constants.ManagedByKueueLabelValue,
   349	                        },
   350	                },
   351	                Template: ps.Template,
   352	        }
   353	
   354	        // set the controller reference to workload so that the template is not left orphaned
   355	        // if the ProvisioningRequest creation fails. The ownership is later transferred to the
   356	        // ProvisioningRequest.
   357	        if err := ctrl.SetControllerReference(wl, newPt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
   358	                return nil, err
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        // apply the admission node selectors to the Template
   362	        psi, err := podset.FromAssignment(ctx, c.client, psa, ptr.Deref(psa.Count, ps.Count))
   363	        if err != nil {
   364	                return nil, err
   365	        }
   366	
   367	        err = podset.Merge(&newPt.Template.ObjectMeta, &newPt.Template.Spec, psi)
   368	        if err != nil {
   369	                return nil, err
   370	        }
   371	
   372	        // copy limits to requests if needed
   373	        workload.UseLimitsAsMissingRequestsInPod(&newPt.Template.Spec)
   374	
   375	        if err := c.client.Create(ctx, newPt); err != nil {
   376	                return nil, err
   377	        }
   378	
   379	        return newPt, nil
   380	}
   381	
   382	func (c *Controller) syncProvisionRequestsPodTemplates(ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload, request *autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest) error {
   383	        for i := range request.Spec.PodSets {
   384	                reqPS := &request.Spec.PodSets[i]
   385	
   386	                pt := &corev1.PodTemplate{}
   387	                ptKey := types.NamespacedName{
   388	                        Namespace: request.Namespace,
   389	                        Name:      reqPS.PodTemplateRef.Name,
   390	                }
   391	
   392	                err := c.client.Get(ctx, ptKey, pt)
   393	                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
   394	                        return err
   395	                }
   396	
   397	                if err == nil {
   398	                        var shouldUpdate bool
   399	
   400	                        // transfer the ownership of the template to the ProvisioningRequest
   401	                        if metav1.IsControlledBy(pt, wl) {
   402	                                if err := controllerutil.RemoveControllerReference(wl, pt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
   403	                                        return err
   404	                                }
   405	                                shouldUpdate = true
   406	                        }
   407	
   408	                        if !metav1.IsControlledBy(pt, request) {
   409	                                if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(request, pt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
   410	                                        return err
   411	                                }
   412	                                shouldUpdate = true
   413	                        }
   414	
   415	                        if shouldUpdate {
   416	                                if err := c.client.Update(ctx, pt); err != nil {
   417	                                        return err
   418	                                }
   419	                        }
   420	                }
   421	        }
   422	        return nil
   423	}
   424	
   425	func (c *Controller) reqIsNeeded(wl *kueue.Workload, prc *kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig) bool {
   426	        return len(requiredPodSets(wl.Spec.PodSets, prc.Spec.ManagedResources)) > 0
   427	}
   428	
   429	func requiredPodSets(podSets []kueue.PodSet, resources []corev1.ResourceName) []kueue.PodSetReference {
   430	        resourcesSet := sets.New(resources...)
   431	        users := make([]kueue.PodSetReference, 0, len(podSets))
   432	        for i := range podSets {
   433	                ps := &podSets[i]
   434	                if len(resources) == 0 || podUses(&ps.Template.Spec, resourcesSet) {
   435	                        users = append(users, ps.Name)
   436	                }
   437	        }
   438	        return users
   439	}
   440	
   441	func podUses(pod *corev1.PodSpec, resourceSet sets.Set[corev1.ResourceName]) bool {
   442	        for i := range pod.InitContainers {
   443	                if containerUses(&pod.InitContainers[i], resourceSet) {
   444	                        return true
   445	                }
   446	        }
   447	        for i := range pod.Containers {
   448	                if containerUses(&pod.Containers[i], resourceSet) {
   449	                        return true
   450	                }
   451	        }
   452	        return false
   453	}
   454	
   455	func containerUses(cont *corev1.Container, resourceSet sets.Set[corev1.ResourceName]) bool {
   456	        for r := range cont.Resources.Requests {
   457	                if resourceSet.Has(r) {
   458	                        return true
   459	                }
   460	        }
   461	        for r := range cont.Resources.Limits {
   462	                if resourceSet.Has(r) {
   463	                        return true
   464	                }
   465	        }
   466	        return false
   467	}
   468	
   469	func updateCheckMessage(checkState *kueue.AdmissionCheckState, message string) bool {
   470	        if message == "" || checkState.Message == message {
   471	                return false
   472	        }
   473	        checkState.Message = message
   474	        return true
   475	}
   476	
   477	func updateCheckState(checkState *kueue.AdmissionCheckState, state kueue.CheckState) bool {
   478	        if checkState.State == state {
   479	                return false
   480	        }
   481	        checkState.State = state
   482	        return true
   483	}
   484	
   485	func (wlInfo *workloadInfo) update(wl *kueue.Workload, c clock.Clock) {
   486	        for _, check := range wl.Status.AdmissionChecks {
   487	                workload.SetAdmissionCheckState(&wlInfo.checkStates, check, c)
   488	        }
   489	        wlInfo.requeueState = wl.Status.RequeueState
   490	}

   618	func podSetUpdates(log logr.Logger, wl *kueue.Workload, pr *autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest, prc *kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig) []kueue.PodSetUpdate {
   619	        podSets := wl.Spec.PodSets
   620	        refMap := slices.ToMap(podSets, func(i int) (string, kueue.PodSetReference) {
   621	                return getProvisioningRequestPodTemplateName(pr.Name, podSets[i].Name), podSets[i].Name
   622	        })
   623	        return slices.Map(pr.Spec.PodSets, func(ps *autoscaling.PodSet) kueue.PodSetUpdate {
   624	                podSetUpdate := kueue.PodSetUpdate{
   625	                        Name: refMap[ps.PodTemplateRef.Name],
   626	                        Annotations: map[string]string{
   627	                                ConsumesAnnotationKey:  pr.Name,
   628	                                ClassNameAnnotationKey: pr.Spec.ProvisioningClassName},
   629	                }
   630	                if psUpdate := prc.Spec.PodSetUpdates; psUpdate != nil {
   631	                        podSetUpdate.NodeSelector = make(map[string]string, len(psUpdate.NodeSelector))
   632	                        for _, nodeSelector := range psUpdate.NodeSelector {
   633	                                value, ok := pr.Status.ProvisioningClassDetails[nodeSelector.ValueFromProvisioningClassDetail]
   634	                                if !ok {
   635	                                        log.Info("skipping detail not found in the ProvisioningClassDetails", "detail", nodeSelector.ValueFromProvisioningClassDetail)
   636	                                        continue
   637	                                }
   638	                                podSetUpdate.NodeSelector[nodeSelector.Key] = string(value)
   639	                        }
   640	                }
   641	                return podSetUpdate
   642	        })
   643	}

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"strings"

	provisioning "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("=== Verifying Deprecated Annotation Removal ===\n")
	
	allGood := true
	
	// Test 1: Verify new constants exist with correct values
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Checking new annotation constants...")
	expectedConsumes := "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/consume-provisioning-request"
	expectedClassName := "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/provisioning-class-name"
	
	if provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey != expectedConsumes {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ConsumesAnnotationKey mismatch.\n    Expected: %s\n    Got: %s\n", expectedConsumes, provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey)
		allGood = false
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: ConsumesAnnotationKey = %s\n", provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey)
	}
	
	if provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey != expectedClassName {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ClassNameAnnotationKey mismatch.\n    Expected: %s\n    Got: %s\n", expectedClassName, provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey)
		allGood = false
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: ClassNameAnnotationKey = %s\n", provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey)
	}
	
	// Test 2: Verify deprecated constants are NOT in the new annotation values
	fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Verifying new annotations don'"'"'t contain deprecated prefix...")
	deprecatedPrefix := "cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io"
	newPrefix := "autoscaling.x-k8s.io"
	
	if strings.Contains(provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey, deprecatedPrefix) {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ConsumesAnnotationKey still contains deprecated prefix '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", deprecatedPrefix)
		allGood = false
	} else if strings.Contains(provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey, newPrefix) {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: ConsumesAnnotationKey uses new prefix '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", newPrefix)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ConsumesAnnotationKey doesn'"'"'t use expected prefix\n")
		allGood = false
	}
	
	if strings.Contains(provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey, deprecatedPrefix) {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ClassNameAnnotationKey still contains deprecated prefix '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", deprecatedPrefix)
		allGood = false
	} else if strings.Contains(provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey, newPrefix) {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: ClassNameAnnotationKey uses new prefix '"'"'%s'"'"'\n", newPrefix)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ClassNameAnnotationKey doesn'"'"'t use expected prefix\n")
		allGood = false
	}
	
	// Test 3: Other constants should still exist
	fmt.Println("\nTest 3: Verifying other constants are preserved...")
	if provisioning.ConfigKind != "ProvisioningRequestConfig" {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: ConfigKind changed unexpectedly: %s\n", provisioning.ConfigKind)
		allGood = false
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: ConfigKind = %s\n", provisioning.ConfigKind)
	}
	
	if provisioning.CheckInactiveMessage != "the check is not active" {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: CheckInactiveMessage changed unexpectedly: %s\n", provisioning.CheckInactiveMessage)
		allGood = false
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: CheckInactiveMessage preserved\n")
	}
	
	if provisioning.NoRequestNeeded != "the provisioning request is not needed" {
		fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: NoRequestNeeded changed unexpectedly: %s\n", provisioning.NoRequestNeeded)
		allGood = false
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("  ✓ PASS: NoRequestNeeded preserved\n")
	}
	
	// Summary
	fmt.Println("\n=== Summary ===")
	if allGood {
		fmt.Println("✓ All tests passed! Deprecated annotations have been successfully removed.")
		os.Exit(0)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Some tests failed. Please review the output above.")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
}

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/CHANGES_SUMMARY.md --file_text '# Summary of Changes: Remove Deprecated ProvisioningRequest Annotations

## Overview
This change removes the deprecated ProvisioningRequest annotations from the Kueue codebase, as per the PR description. The deprecated annotations used the `cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io` prefix and have been superseded by new annotations using the `autoscaling.x-k8s.io` prefix.

## Files Modified

### 1. `/testbed/pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/constants.go`
**Changes:**
- Removed `DeprecatedConsumesAnnotationKey` constant (value: `"cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/consume-provisioning-request"`)
- Removed `DeprecatedClassNameAnnotationKey` constant (value: `"cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/provisioning-class-name"`)
- Kept the new annotation constants:
  - `ConsumesAnnotationKey` = `"autoscaling.x-k8s.io/consume-provisioning-request"`
  - `ClassNameAnnotationKey` = `"autoscaling.x-k8s.io/provisioning-class-name"`

**Before:**
```go
const (
        ConfigKind                       = "ProvisioningRequestConfig"
        DeprecatedConsumesAnnotationKey  = "cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/consume-provisioning-request"
        DeprecatedClassNameAnnotationKey = "cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/provisioning-class-name"
        ConsumesAnnotationKey            = "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/consume-provisioning-request"
        ClassNameAnnotationKey           = "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/provisioning-class-name"

        CheckInactiveMessage = "the check is not active"
        NoRequestNeeded      = "the provisioning request is not needed"
)
```

**After:**
```go
const (
        ConfigKind             = "ProvisioningRequestConfig"
        ConsumesAnnotationKey  = "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/consume-provisioning-request"
        ClassNameAnnotationKey = "autoscaling.x-k8s.io/provisioning-class-name"

        CheckInactiveMessage = "the check is not active"
        NoRequestNeeded      = "the provisioning request is not needed"
)
```

### 2. `/testbed/pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/controller.go`
**Changes:**
- Removed usage of deprecated annotation constants in the `podSetUpdates` function
- Now only sets the new annotations (not both old and new)

**Before (lines 623-631):**
```go
return slices.Map(pr.Spec.PodSets, func(ps *autoscaling.PodSet) kueue.PodSetUpdate {
        podSetUpdate := kueue.PodSetUpdate{
                Name: refMap[ps.PodTemplateRef.Name],
                Annotations: map[string]string{
                        DeprecatedConsumesAnnotationKey:  pr.Name,
                        DeprecatedClassNameAnnotationKey: pr.Spec.ProvisioningClassName,
                        ConsumesAnnotationKey:            pr.Name,
                        ClassNameAnnotationKey:           pr.Spec.ProvisioningClassName},
        }
```

**After (lines 623-629):**
```go
return slices.Map(pr.Spec.PodSets, func(ps *autoscaling.PodSet) kueue.PodSetUpdate {
        podSetUpdate := kueue.PodSetUpdate{
                Name: refMap[ps.PodTemplateRef.Name],
                Annotations: map[string]string{
                        ConsumesAnnotationKey:  pr.Name,
                        ClassNameAnnotationKey: pr.Spec.ProvisioningClassName},
        }
```

## Impact

### What Changed
1. The deprecated constants are no longer defined in the codebase
2. The code now only sets the new annotations on PodSetUpdate objects
3. Old ClusterAutoscaler versions expecting the deprecated annotations will no longer receive them

### What Stayed the Same
- All other constants remain unchanged (ConfigKind, CheckInactiveMessage, NoRequestNeeded)
- The new annotation constants and their values remain unchanged
- The overall logic and behavior of the provisioning controller remains the same
- Only the annotation keys have been updated

## Verification

The changes have been verified by:
1. Successfully compiling the modified package
2. Confirming no deprecated annotation strings remain in non-test code
3. Verifying the new annotation constants have the correct values
4. Ensuring all other constants are preserved

## Backward Compatibility Note

This is a **breaking change** for older ClusterAutoscaler versions that rely on the deprecated annotations. Users must upgrade their ClusterAutoscaler to a version that supports the new `autoscaling.x-k8s.io/*` annotations before using this version of Kueue.
'

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_annotation_behavior.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"reflect"

	provisioning "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("=== Testing Annotation Behavior ===\n")
	
	// Simulate what annotations would be set in a PodSetUpdate
	annotations := make(map[string]string)
	
	// Using the constants as they would be used in the actual code
	prName := "test-provisioning-request"
	className := "test-class"
	
	annotations[provisioning.ConsumesAnnotationKey] = prName
	annotations[provisioning.ClassNameAnnotationKey] = className
	
	fmt.Println("Annotations that would be set on PodSetUpdate:")
	for key, value := range annotations {
		fmt.Printf("  %s: %s\n", key, value)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nExpected annotations:")
	expected := map[string]string{
		"autoscaling.x-k8s.io/consume-provisioning-request": prName,
		"autoscaling.x-k8s.io/provisioning-class-name":      className,
	}
	
	for key, value := range expected {
		fmt.Printf("  %s: %s\n", key, value)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nVerifying annotations match expected:")
	if reflect.DeepEqual(annotations, expected) {
		fmt.Println("  ✓ PASS: Annotations match expected values")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("  ✗ FAIL: Annotations do not match expected values")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nVerifying NO deprecated annotations are present:")
	deprecatedKeys := []string{
		"cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/consume-provisioning-request",
		"cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/provisioning-class-name",
	}
	
	hasDeprecated := false
	for _, key := range deprecatedKeys {
		if _, exists := annotations[key]; exists {
			fmt.Printf("  ✗ FAIL: Found deprecated annotation: %s\n", key)
			hasDeprecated = true
		}
	}
	
	if !hasDeprecated {
		fmt.Println("  ✓ PASS: No deprecated annotations present")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n=== Test Complete ===")
}
'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/final_verification.sh --file_text '#!/bin/bash

echo "==================================================================="
echo "  Final Verification: Deprecated Annotations Removal"
echo "==================================================================="
echo ""

# Colors
GREEN='"'"'\033[0;32m'"'"'
RED='"'"'\033[0;31m'"'"'
NC='"'"'\033[0m'"'"' # No Color

PASS=0
FAIL=0

# Test 1: Check that deprecated constants are not defined in constants.go
echo "Test 1: Checking that deprecated constants are not defined..."
if grep -q "DeprecatedConsumesAnnotationKey\|DeprecatedClassNameAnnotationKey" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/constants.go; then
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: Deprecated constants still exist in constants.go"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
else
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: Deprecated constants removed from constants.go"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
fi

# Test 2: Check that deprecated constants are not used in controller.go
echo "Test 2: Checking that deprecated constants are not used in controller.go..."
if grep -q "DeprecatedConsumesAnnotationKey\|DeprecatedClassNameAnnotationKey" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/controller.go; then
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: Deprecated constants still used in controller.go"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
else
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: Deprecated constants not used in controller.go"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
fi

# Test 3: Check that new constants are defined
echo "Test 3: Checking that new constants are defined..."
if grep -q "ConsumesAnnotationKey.*autoscaling.x-k8s.io" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/constants.go && \
   grep -q "ClassNameAnnotationKey.*autoscaling.x-k8s.io" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/constants.go; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: New constants are properly defined"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
else
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: New constants are not properly defined"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
fi

# Test 4: Check that new constants are used in controller.go
echo "Test 4: Checking that new constants are used in controller.go..."
if grep -q "ConsumesAnnotationKey:" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/controller.go && \
   grep -q "ClassNameAnnotationKey:" pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/controller.go; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: New constants are used in controller.go"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
else
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: New constants are not used in controller.go"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
fi

# Test 5: Check that deprecated annotation strings don'"'"'t exist in non-test code
echo "Test 5: Checking for deprecated annotation strings in non-test code..."
DEPRECATED_FOUND=$(find pkg -name "*.go" ! -name "*_test.go" -type f -exec grep -l "cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/consume-provisioning-request\|cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/provisioning-class-name" {} \; 2>/dev/null | wc -l)
if [ "$DEPRECATED_FOUND" -eq 0 ]; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: No deprecated annotation strings in non-test code"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
else
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: Found $DEPRECATED_FOUND file(s) with deprecated annotation strings"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
fi

# Test 6: Check that the code compiles
echo "Test 6: Checking that the code compiles..."
if go build ./pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/... >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: Code compiles successfully"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
else
    echo -e "${RED}✗ FAIL${NC}: Code does not compile"
    FAIL=$((FAIL+1))
fi

# Test 7: Verify ConfigKind constant is preserved
echo "Test 7: Checking that other constants are preserved..."
if grep -q '"'"'ConfigKind.*=.*"ProvisioningRequestConfig"'"'"' pkg/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/constants.go; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}✓ PASS${NC}: Other constants are preserved"
    PASS=$((PASS+1))
else

    exit 0

    exit 1

+
+        // get the lists of relevant checks
+        relevantChecks, err := admissioncheck.FilterForController(ctx, c.client, wl.Status.AdmissionChecks, kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName)
+        if err != nil {
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        checkConfig := make(map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig, len(relevantChecks))
+        for _, checkName := range relevantChecks {
+                prc, err := c.helper.ConfigForAdmissionCheck(ctx, checkName)
+                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
+                        return reconcile.Result{}, err
+                }
+                checkConfig[checkName] = prc
+        }
+
+        activeOrLastPRForChecks := c.activeOrLastPRForChecks(ctx, wl, checkConfig, provReqs.Items)
+
+        wlInfo := workloadInfo{
+                checkStates: make([]kueue.AdmissionCheckState, 0),
+        }
+        err = c.syncCheckStates(ctx, wl, &wlInfo, checkConfig, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
+        if err != nil {
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        err = c.deleteUnusedProvisioningRequests(ctx, provReqs.Items, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
+        if err != nil {
+                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed to delete unused provisioning requests")
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        err = c.syncOwnedProvisionRequest(ctx, wl, &wlInfo, checkConfig, activeOrLastPRForChecks)
+        if err != nil {
+                // this can also delete unneeded checks
+                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed")
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
 }

-	ctx context.Context, wl *kueue.Workload,

-	checkConfig map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig,
-	activeOrLastPRForChecks map[kueue.AdmissionCheckReference]*autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest,

   618	func podSetUpdates(log logr.Logger, wl *kueue.Workload, pr *autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest, prc *kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig) []kueue.PodSetUpdate {
   619	        podSets := wl.Spec.PodSets
   620	        refMap := slices.ToMap(podSets, func(i int) (string, kueue.PodSetReference) {
   621	                return getProvisioningRequestPodTemplateName(pr.Name, podSets[i].Name), podSets[i].Name
   622	        })
   623	        return slices.Map(pr.Spec.PodSets, func(ps *autoscaling.PodSet) kueue.PodSetUpdate {
   624	                podSetUpdate := kueue.PodSetUpdate{
   625	                        Name: refMap[ps.PodTemplateRef.Name],
   626	                        Annotations: map[string]string{
   627	                                ConsumesAnnotationKey:  pr.Name,
   628	                                ClassNameAnnotationKey: pr.Spec.ProvisioningClassName},
   629	                }
   630	                if psUpdate := prc.Spec.PodSetUpdates; psUpdate != nil {
   631	                        podSetUpdate.NodeSelector = make(map[string]string, len(psUpdate.NodeSelector))
   632	                        for _, nodeSelector := range psUpdate.NodeSelector {
   633	                                value, ok := pr.Status.ProvisioningClassDetails[nodeSelector.ValueFromProvisioningClassDetail]
   634	                                if !ok {
   635	                                        log.Info("skipping detail not found in the ProvisioningClassDetails", "detail", nodeSelector.ValueFromProvisioningClassDetail)
   636	                                        continue
   637	                                }
   638	                                podSetUpdate.NodeSelector[nodeSelector.Key] = string(value)
   639	                        }
   640	                }
   641	                return podSetUpdate
   642	        })
   643	}

 // Result.Requeue is true, otherwise upon completion it will remove the work from the queue.

+                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed")
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }

+        return reconcile.Result{}, nil

+        // if the ProvisioningRequest creation fails. The ownership is later transferred to the
+        // ProvisioningRequest.
+        if err := ctrl.SetControllerReference(wl, newPt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // apply the admission node selectors to the Template
+        psi, err := podset.FromAssignment(ctx, c.client, psa, ptr.Deref(psa.Count, ps.Count))
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        err = podset.Merge(&newPt.Template.ObjectMeta, &newPt.Template.Spec, psi)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // copy limits to requests if needed
+        workload.UseLimitsAsMissingRequestsInPod(&newPt.Template.Spec)
+
+        if err := c.client.Create(ctx, newPt); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        return newPt, nil
 }

 // Reconcile performs a full reconciliation for the object referred to by the Request.
 // The Controller will requeue the Request to be processed again if an error is non-nil or
 // Result.Requeue is true, otherwise upon completion it will remove the work from the queue.

+        provReqs := &autoscaling.ProvisioningRequestList{}

+
+        // get the lists of relevant checks
+        relevantChecks, err := admissioncheck.FilterForController(ctx, c.client, wl.Status.AdmissionChecks, kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName)
+        if err != nil {
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+

+        for _, checkName := range relevantChecks {
+                prc, err := c.helper.ConfigForAdmissionCheck(ctx, checkName)
+                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
+                        return reconcile.Result{}, err
+                }
+                checkConfig[checkName] = prc
+        }
+
+        activeOrLastPRForChecks := c.activeOrLastPRForChecks(ctx, wl, checkConfig, provReqs.Items)
+
+        wlInfo := workloadInfo{
+                checkStates: make([]kueue.AdmissionCheckState, 0),
+        }

+        if err != nil {

+        }

+        if err != nil {
+                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed to delete unused provisioning requests")
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+

+        if err != nil {
+                // this can also delete unneeded checks
+                log.V(2).Error(err, "syncOwnedProvisionRequest failed")
+                return reconcile.Result{}, err
+        }
+
+        return reconcile.Result{}, nil
 }

+        // set the controller reference to workload so that the template is not left orphaned
+        // if the ProvisioningRequest creation fails. The ownership is later transferred to the
+        // ProvisioningRequest.
+        if err := ctrl.SetControllerReference(wl, newPt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // apply the admission node selectors to the Template
+        psi, err := podset.FromAssignment(ctx, c.client, psa, ptr.Deref(psa.Count, ps.Count))
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        err = podset.Merge(&newPt.Template.ObjectMeta, &newPt.Template.Spec, psi)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // copy limits to requests if needed
+        workload.UseLimitsAsMissingRequestsInPod(&newPt.Template.Spec)
+
+        if err := c.client.Create(ctx, newPt); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        return newPt, nil
 }

+                        Namespace: request.Namespace,
+                        Name:      reqPS.PodTemplateRef.Name,
+                }

+                if client.IgnoreNotFound(err) != nil {
+                        return err
+                }

+
+                        // transfer the ownership of the template to the ProvisioningRequest
+                        if metav1.IsControlledBy(pt, wl) {
+                                if err := controllerutil.RemoveControllerReference(wl, pt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
+                                        return err
+                                }
+                                shouldUpdate = true
+                        }
+
+                        if !metav1.IsControlledBy(pt, request) {
+                                if err := controllerutil.SetControllerReference(request, pt, c.client.Scheme()); err != nil {
+                                        return err
+                                }
+                                shouldUpdate = true
+                        }
+
+                        if shouldUpdate {
+                                if err := c.client.Update(ctx, pt); err != nil {
+                                        return err
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        return nil
